<h2 id="examples" class="fs_1.5em mt_2em mb_1em lh_1.3333333 fw_700 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_800 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.875em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#examples"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Examples</h2>
<div class="d_flex flex-d_column gap_0 not-prose [&amp;_&gt;_.example-preview-scope]:bdr-b_0"><div class="d_flex min-h_32 md:min-h_48 bg_bg.default bdr_lg bd-w_1px w_full ov_hidden not-prose example-preview-scope"><div class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_center jc_center flex_1 p_4 md:p_6 w_full"><div class="example-spinner" role="status" aria-label="Loading example"></div></div></div><div data-scope="collapsible" data-part="root" data-state="closed" dir="ltr" id="collapsible:_R_gbhanpfn5tlb_"><button class="button button--variant_outline button--size_xs bd-c_inherit c_fg.default w_full bdr-t_0 bd-t-w_0 bg_bg.default c_fg.muted fw_medium fs_xs gap_1.5 hover:bg_gray.2 hover:c_fg.default" data-scope="collapsible" data-part="trigger" id="collapsible:_R_gbhanpfn5tlb_:trigger" dir="ltr" type="button" data-state="closed" aria-controls="collapsible:_R_gbhanpfn5tlb_:content" aria-expanded="false"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-code icon icon--size_sm" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m16 18 6-6-6-6"></path><path d="m8 6-6 6 6 6"></path></svg>Show Code</button></div></div>
<h3 id="controlled" class="fs_1.25em lh_1.6 mt_1.6em mb_0.6em fw_600 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_700 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.9em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#controlled"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Controlled</h3>
<p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500">Manage the dialog state using the <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">open</code> and <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">onOpenChange</code> props.</p>
<div class="d_flex flex-d_column gap_0 not-prose [&amp;_&gt;_.example-preview-scope]:bdr-b_0"><div class="d_flex min-h_32 md:min-h_48 bg_bg.default bdr_lg bd-w_1px w_full ov_hidden not-prose example-preview-scope"><div class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_center jc_center flex_1 p_4 md:p_6 w_full"><div class="example-spinner" role="status" aria-label="Loading example"></div></div></div><div data-scope="collapsible" data-part="root" data-state="closed" dir="ltr" id="collapsible:_R_ghhanpfn5tlb_"><button class="button button--variant_outline button--size_xs bd-c_inherit c_fg.default w_full bdr-t_0 bd-t-w_0 bg_bg.default c_fg.muted fw_medium fs_xs gap_1.5 hover:bg_gray.2 hover:c_fg.default" data-scope="collapsible" data-part="trigger" id="collapsible:_R_ghhanpfn5tlb_:trigger" dir="ltr" type="button" data-state="closed" aria-controls="collapsible:_R_ghhanpfn5tlb_:content" aria-expanded="false"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-code icon icon--size_sm" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m16 18 6-6-6-6"></path><path d="m8 6-6 6 6 6"></path></svg>Show Code</button></div></div>
<h3 id="root-provider" class="fs_1.25em lh_1.6 mt_1.6em mb_0.6em fw_600 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_700 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.9em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#root-provider"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Root Provider</h3>
<p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500">An alternative way to control the dialog is to use the <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">RootProvider</code> component and the <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">useDialog</code> hook. This way you
can access the state and methods from outside the component.</p>
<div class="d_flex flex-d_column gap_0 not-prose [&amp;_&gt;_.example-preview-scope]:bdr-b_0"><div class="d_flex min-h_32 md:min-h_48 bg_bg.default bdr_lg bd-w_1px w_full ov_hidden not-prose example-preview-scope"><div class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_center jc_center flex_1 p_4 md:p_6 w_full"><div class="example-spinner" role="status" aria-label="Loading example"></div></div></div><div data-scope="collapsible" data-part="root" data-state="closed" dir="ltr" id="collapsible:_R_gnhanpfn5tlb_"><button class="button button--variant_outline button--size_xs bd-c_inherit c_fg.default w_full bdr-t_0 bd-t-w_0 bg_bg.default c_fg.muted fw_medium fs_xs gap_1.5 hover:bg_gray.2 hover:c_fg.default" data-scope="collapsible" data-part="trigger" id="collapsible:_R_gnhanpfn5tlb_:trigger" dir="ltr" type="button" data-state="closed" aria-controls="collapsible:_R_gnhanpfn5tlb_:content" aria-expanded="false"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-code icon icon--size_sm" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m16 18 6-6-6-6"></path><path d="m8 6-6 6 6 6"></path></svg>Show Code</button></div></div>
<h3 id="alert-dialog" class="fs_1.25em lh_1.6 mt_1.6em mb_0.6em fw_600 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_700 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.9em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#alert-dialog"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Alert Dialog</h3>
<p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500">For critical confirmations or destructive actions, use <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">role=&quot;alertdialog&quot;</code>. Alert dialogs differ from regular dialogs
in important ways:</p>
<ul class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em ps_1.625em li-t_disc [&amp;_&gt;_li]:ps_0.375em [&amp;_&gt;_li]:[&amp;::marker]:c_fg.subtle [&amp;_&gt;_li_p]:mt_0.75em [&amp;_&gt;_li_p]:mb_0.75em [&amp;_&gt;_li_&gt;_p:first-child]:mt_1.25em [&amp;_&gt;_li_&gt;_p:last-child]:mb_1.25em [&amp;_ul,_&amp;_ol]:mt_0.75em [&amp;_ul,_&amp;_ol]:mb_0.75em">
<li class="mt_0.5em mb_0.5em"><strong class="c_var(--colors-prose-bold) fw_600">Automatic focus</strong>: The close/cancel button receives focus when opened, prioritizing the safest action</li>
<li class="mt_0.5em mb_0.5em"><strong class="c_var(--colors-prose-bold) fw_600">Requires explicit dismissal</strong>: Cannot be closed by clicking outside, only via button clicks or Escape key</li>
</ul>
<div class="d_flex flex-d_column gap_0 not-prose [&amp;_&gt;_.example-preview-scope]:bdr-b_0"><div class="d_flex min-h_32 md:min-h_48 bg_bg.default bdr_lg bd-w_1px w_full ov_hidden not-prose example-preview-scope"><div class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_center jc_center flex_1 p_4 md:p_6 w_full"><div class="example-spinner" role="status" aria-label="Loading example"></div></div></div><div data-scope="collapsible" data-part="root" data-state="closed" dir="ltr" id="collapsible:_R_gvhanpfn5tlb_"><button class="button button--variant_outline button--size_xs bd-c_inherit c_fg.default w_full bdr-t_0 bd-t-w_0 bg_bg.default c_fg.muted fw_medium fs_xs gap_1.5 hover:bg_gray.2 hover:c_fg.default" data-scope="collapsible" data-part="trigger" id="collapsible:_R_gvhanpfn5tlb_:trigger" dir="ltr" type="button" data-state="closed" aria-controls="collapsible:_R_gvhanpfn5tlb_:content" aria-expanded="false"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-code icon icon--size_sm" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m16 18 6-6-6-6"></path><path d="m8 6-6 6 6 6"></path></svg>Show Code</button></div></div>
<h3 id="lazy-mount" class="fs_1.25em lh_1.6 mt_1.6em mb_0.6em fw_600 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_700 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.9em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#lazy-mount"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Lazy Mount</h3>
<p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500">Use <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">lazyMount</code> to render dialog content only when first opened. Combine with <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">unmountOnExit</code> to unmount when closed,
freeing up resources.</p>
<div class="d_flex flex-d_column gap_0 not-prose [&amp;_&gt;_.example-preview-scope]:bdr-b_0"><div class="d_flex min-h_32 md:min-h_48 bg_bg.default bdr_lg bd-w_1px w_full ov_hidden not-prose example-preview-scope"><div class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_center jc_center flex_1 p_4 md:p_6 w_full"><div class="example-spinner" role="status" aria-label="Loading example"></div></div></div><div data-scope="collapsible" data-part="root" data-state="closed" dir="ltr" id="collapsible:_R_h5hanpfn5tlb_"><button class="button button--variant_outline button--size_xs bd-c_inherit c_fg.default w_full bdr-t_0 bd-t-w_0 bg_bg.default c_fg.muted fw_medium fs_xs gap_1.5 hover:bg_gray.2 hover:c_fg.default" data-scope="collapsible" data-part="trigger" id="collapsible:_R_h5hanpfn5tlb_:trigger" dir="ltr" type="button" data-state="closed" aria-controls="collapsible:_R_h5hanpfn5tlb_:content" aria-expanded="false"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-code icon icon--size_sm" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m16 18 6-6-6-6"></path><path d="m8 6-6 6 6 6"></path></svg>Show Code</button></div></div>
<h3 id="initial-focus" class="fs_1.25em lh_1.6 mt_1.6em mb_0.6em fw_600 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_700 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.9em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#initial-focus"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Initial Focus</h3>
<p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500">Use <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">initialFocusEl</code> to control which element receives focus when the dialog opens.</p>
<div class="d_flex flex-d_column gap_0 not-prose [&amp;_&gt;_.example-preview-scope]:bdr-b_0"><div class="d_flex min-h_32 md:min-h_48 bg_bg.default bdr_lg bd-w_1px w_full ov_hidden not-prose example-preview-scope"><div class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_center jc_center flex_1 p_4 md:p_6 w_full"><div class="example-spinner" role="status" aria-label="Loading example"></div></div></div><div data-scope="collapsible" data-part="root" data-state="closed" dir="ltr" id="collapsible:_R_hbhanpfn5tlb_"><button class="button button--variant_outline button--size_xs bd-c_inherit c_fg.default w_full bdr-t_0 bd-t-w_0 bg_bg.default c_fg.muted fw_medium fs_xs gap_1.5 hover:bg_gray.2 hover:c_fg.default" data-scope="collapsible" data-part="trigger" id="collapsible:_R_hbhanpfn5tlb_:trigger" dir="ltr" type="button" data-state="closed" aria-controls="collapsible:_R_hbhanpfn5tlb_:content" aria-expanded="false"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-code icon icon--size_sm" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m16 18 6-6-6-6"></path><path d="m8 6-6 6 6 6"></path></svg>Show Code</button></div></div>
<h3 id="final-focus" class="fs_1.25em lh_1.6 mt_1.6em mb_0.6em fw_600 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_700 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.9em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#final-focus"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Final Focus</h3>
<p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500">Use <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">finalFocusEl</code> to control which element receives focus when the dialog closes. Defaults to the trigger element.</p>
<div class="d_flex flex-d_column gap_0 not-prose [&amp;_&gt;_.example-preview-scope]:bdr-b_0"><div class="d_flex min-h_32 md:min-h_48 bg_bg.default bdr_lg bd-w_1px w_full ov_hidden not-prose example-preview-scope"><div class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_center jc_center flex_1 p_4 md:p_6 w_full"><div class="example-spinner" role="status" aria-label="Loading example"></div></div></div><div data-scope="collapsible" data-part="root" data-state="closed" dir="ltr" id="collapsible:_R_hhhanpfn5tlb_"><button class="button button--variant_outline button--size_xs bd-c_inherit c_fg.default w_full bdr-t_0 bd-t-w_0 bg_bg.default c_fg.muted fw_medium fs_xs gap_1.5 hover:bg_gray.2 hover:c_fg.default" data-scope="collapsible" data-part="trigger" id="collapsible:_R_hhhanpfn5tlb_:trigger" dir="ltr" type="button" data-state="closed" aria-controls="collapsible:_R_hhhanpfn5tlb_:content" aria-expanded="false"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-code icon icon--size_sm" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m16 18 6-6-6-6"></path><path d="m8 6-6 6 6 6"></path></svg>Show Code</button></div></div>
<h3 id="non-modal" class="fs_1.25em lh_1.6 mt_1.6em mb_0.6em fw_600 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_700 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.9em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#non-modal"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Non-Modal</h3>
<p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500">Use <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">modal={false}</code> to allow interaction with elements outside the dialog. Disables focus trapping and scroll
prevention.</p>
<div class="d_flex flex-d_column gap_0 not-prose [&amp;_&gt;_.example-preview-scope]:bdr-b_0"><div class="d_flex min-h_32 md:min-h_48 bg_bg.default bdr_lg bd-w_1px w_full ov_hidden not-prose example-preview-scope"><div class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_center jc_center flex_1 p_4 md:p_6 w_full"><div class="example-spinner" role="status" aria-label="Loading example"></div></div></div><div data-scope="collapsible" data-part="root" data-state="closed" dir="ltr" id="collapsible:_R_hnhanpfn5tlb_"><button class="button button--variant_outline button--size_xs bd-c_inherit c_fg.default w_full bdr-t_0 bd-t-w_0 bg_bg.default c_fg.muted fw_medium fs_xs gap_1.5 hover:bg_gray.2 hover:c_fg.default" data-scope="collapsible" data-part="trigger" id="collapsible:_R_hnhanpfn5tlb_:trigger" dir="ltr" type="button" data-state="closed" aria-controls="collapsible:_R_hnhanpfn5tlb_:content" aria-expanded="false"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-code icon icon--size_sm" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m16 18 6-6-6-6"></path><path d="m8 6-6 6 6 6"></path></svg>Show Code</button></div></div>
<h3 id="inside-scroll" class="fs_1.25em lh_1.6 mt_1.6em mb_0.6em fw_600 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_700 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.9em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#inside-scroll"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Inside Scroll</h3>
<p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500">Make the content area scrollable while keeping header and footer fixed using <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">maxHeight</code> and <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">overflow: auto</code>.</p>
<div class="d_flex flex-d_column gap_0 not-prose [&amp;_&gt;_.example-preview-scope]:bdr-b_0"><div class="d_flex min-h_32 md:min-h_48 bg_bg.default bdr_lg bd-w_1px w_full ov_hidden not-prose example-preview-scope"><div class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_center jc_center flex_1 p_4 md:p_6 w_full"><div class="example-spinner" role="status" aria-label="Loading example"></div></div></div><div data-scope="collapsible" data-part="root" data-state="closed" dir="ltr" id="collapsible:_R_hthanpfn5tlb_"><button class="button button--variant_outline button--size_xs bd-c_inherit c_fg.default w_full bdr-t_0 bd-t-w_0 bg_bg.default c_fg.muted fw_medium fs_xs gap_1.5 hover:bg_gray.2 hover:c_fg.default" data-scope="collapsible" data-part="trigger" id="collapsible:_R_hthanpfn5tlb_:trigger" dir="ltr" type="button" data-state="closed" aria-controls="collapsible:_R_hthanpfn5tlb_:content" aria-expanded="false"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-code icon icon--size_sm" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m16 18 6-6-6-6"></path><path d="m8 6-6 6 6 6"></path></svg>Show Code</button></div></div>
<h3 id="outside-scroll" class="fs_1.25em lh_1.6 mt_1.6em mb_0.6em fw_600 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_700 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.9em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#outside-scroll"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Outside Scroll</h3>
<p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500">Make the positioner scrollable so the dialog can extend beyond the viewport.</p>
<div class="d_flex flex-d_column gap_0 not-prose [&amp;_&gt;_.example-preview-scope]:bdr-b_0"><div class="d_flex min-h_32 md:min-h_48 bg_bg.default bdr_lg bd-w_1px w_full ov_hidden not-prose example-preview-scope"><div class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_center jc_center flex_1 p_4 md:p_6 w_full"><div class="example-spinner" role="status" aria-label="Loading example"></div></div></div><div data-scope="collapsible" data-part="root" data-state="closed" dir="ltr" id="collapsible:_R_i3hanpfn5tlb_"><button class="button button--variant_outline button--size_xs bd-c_inherit c_fg.default w_full bdr-t_0 bd-t-w_0 bg_bg.default c_fg.muted fw_medium fs_xs gap_1.5 hover:bg_gray.2 hover:c_fg.default" data-scope="collapsible" data-part="trigger" id="collapsible:_R_i3hanpfn5tlb_:trigger" dir="ltr" type="button" data-state="closed" aria-controls="collapsible:_R_i3hanpfn5tlb_:content" aria-expanded="false"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-code icon icon--size_sm" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m16 18 6-6-6-6"></path><path d="m8 6-6 6 6 6"></path></svg>Show Code</button></div></div>
<h3 id="context" class="fs_1.25em lh_1.6 mt_1.6em mb_0.6em fw_600 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_700 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.9em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#context"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Context</h3>
<p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500">Access the dialog&#x27;s state and methods with <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">Dialog.Context</code> or the <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">useDialogContext</code> hook.</p>
<div class="d_flex flex-d_column gap_0 not-prose [&amp;_&gt;_.example-preview-scope]:bdr-b_0"><div class="d_flex min-h_32 md:min-h_48 bg_bg.default bdr_lg bd-w_1px w_full ov_hidden not-prose example-preview-scope"><div class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_center jc_center flex_1 p_4 md:p_6 w_full"><div class="example-spinner" role="status" aria-label="Loading example"></div></div></div><div data-scope="collapsible" data-part="root" data-state="closed" dir="ltr" id="collapsible:_R_i9hanpfn5tlb_"><button class="button button--variant_outline button--size_xs bd-c_inherit c_fg.default w_full bdr-t_0 bd-t-w_0 bg_bg.default c_fg.muted fw_medium fs_xs gap_1.5 hover:bg_gray.2 hover:c_fg.default" data-scope="collapsible" data-part="trigger" id="collapsible:_R_i9hanpfn5tlb_:trigger" dir="ltr" type="button" data-state="closed" aria-controls="collapsible:_R_i9hanpfn5tlb_:content" aria-expanded="false"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-code icon icon--size_sm" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m16 18 6-6-6-6"></path><path d="m8 6-6 6 6 6"></path></svg>Show Code</button></div></div>
<h3 id="open-from-menu" class="fs_1.25em lh_1.6 mt_1.6em mb_0.6em fw_600 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_700 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.9em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#open-from-menu"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Open from Menu</h3>
<p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500">Open a dialog imperatively from a menu item using the <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">onClick</code> handler.</p>
<div class="d_flex flex-d_column gap_0 not-prose [&amp;_&gt;_.example-preview-scope]:bdr-b_0"><div class="d_flex min-h_32 md:min-h_48 bg_bg.default bdr_lg bd-w_1px w_full ov_hidden not-prose example-preview-scope"><div class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_center jc_center flex_1 p_4 md:p_6 w_full"><div class="example-spinner" role="status" aria-label="Loading example"></div></div></div><div data-scope="collapsible" data-part="root" data-state="closed" dir="ltr" id="collapsible:_R_ifhanpfn5tlb_"><button class="button button--variant_outline button--size_xs bd-c_inherit c_fg.default w_full bdr-t_0 bd-t-w_0 bg_bg.default c_fg.muted fw_medium fs_xs gap_1.5 hover:bg_gray.2 hover:c_fg.default" data-scope="collapsible" data-part="trigger" id="collapsible:_R_ifhanpfn5tlb_:trigger" dir="ltr" type="button" data-state="closed" aria-controls="collapsible:_R_ifhanpfn5tlb_:content" aria-expanded="false"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-code icon icon--size_sm" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m16 18 6-6-6-6"></path><path d="m8 6-6 6 6 6"></path></svg>Show Code</button></div></div>
<h3 id="nested" class="fs_1.25em lh_1.6 mt_1.6em mb_0.6em fw_600 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_700 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.9em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#nested"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Nested</h3>
<p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500">Nest dialogs within one another. The parent receives <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">data-has-nested</code> and <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">--nested-layer-count</code> CSS variable for
styling effects like zoom-out:</p>
<pre class="fs_0.875em lh_1.7142857 mt_1.7142857em mb_1.7142857em bdr_0.375rem p_4 color-scheme_dark [&amp;_code]:bg-c_transparent [&amp;_code]:bd-w_0 [&amp;_code]:bdr_0 [&amp;_code]:p_0 [&amp;_code]:fw_inherit [&amp;_code]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_inherit [&amp;_code]:ff_inherit [&amp;_code]:lh_inherit shiki github-dark-default" style="background-color:#0d1117;color:#e6edf3" tabindex="0"><code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2"><span class="line"><span style="color:#E6EDF3">[</span><span style="color:#79C0FF">data-part</span><span style="color:#FF7B72">=</span><span style="color:#A5D6FF">&#x27;content&#x27;</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">][</span><span style="color:#79C0FF">data-has-nested</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">] {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#79C0FF">  transform</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">: </span><span style="color:#79C0FF">scale</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">(</span><span style="color:#79C0FF">calc</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">(</span><span style="color:#79C0FF">1</span><span style="color:#FF7B72"> -</span><span style="color:#79C0FF"> var</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">(</span><span style="color:#FFA657">--nested-layer-count</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">) </span><span style="color:#FF7B72">*</span><span style="color:#79C0FF"> 0.05</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">));</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E6EDF3">}</span></span></code></pre>
<div class="d_flex flex-d_column gap_0 not-prose [&amp;_&gt;_.example-preview-scope]:bdr-b_0"><div class="d_flex min-h_32 md:min-h_48 bg_bg.default bdr_lg bd-w_1px w_full ov_hidden not-prose example-preview-scope"><div class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_center jc_center flex_1 p_4 md:p_6 w_full"><div class="example-spinner" role="status" aria-label="Loading example"></div></div></div><div data-scope="collapsible" data-part="root" data-state="closed" dir="ltr" id="collapsible:_R_inhanpfn5tlb_"><button class="button button--variant_outline button--size_xs bd-c_inherit c_fg.default w_full bdr-t_0 bd-t-w_0 bg_bg.default c_fg.muted fw_medium fs_xs gap_1.5 hover:bg_gray.2 hover:c_fg.default" data-scope="collapsible" data-part="trigger" id="collapsible:_R_inhanpfn5tlb_:trigger" dir="ltr" type="button" data-state="closed" aria-controls="collapsible:_R_inhanpfn5tlb_:content" aria-expanded="false"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-code icon icon--size_sm" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m16 18 6-6-6-6"></path><path d="m8 6-6 6 6 6"></path></svg>Show Code</button></div></div>
<h3 id="confirmation" class="fs_1.25em lh_1.6 mt_1.6em mb_0.6em fw_600 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_700 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.9em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#confirmation"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Confirmation</h3>
<p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500">Intercept close attempts to show confirmation prompts, preventing data loss from unsaved changes.</p>
<div class="d_flex flex-d_column gap_0 not-prose [&amp;_&gt;_.example-preview-scope]:bdr-b_0"><div class="d_flex min-h_32 md:min-h_48 bg_bg.default bdr_lg bd-w_1px w_full ov_hidden not-prose example-preview-scope"><div class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_center jc_center flex_1 p_4 md:p_6 w_full"><div class="example-spinner" role="status" aria-label="Loading example"></div></div></div><div data-scope="collapsible" data-part="root" data-state="closed" dir="ltr" id="collapsible:_R_ithanpfn5tlb_"><button class="button button--variant_outline button--size_xs bd-c_inherit c_fg.default w_full bdr-t_0 bd-t-w_0 bg_bg.default c_fg.muted fw_medium fs_xs gap_1.5 hover:bg_gray.2 hover:c_fg.default" data-scope="collapsible" data-part="trigger" id="collapsible:_R_ithanpfn5tlb_:trigger" dir="ltr" type="button" data-state="closed" aria-controls="collapsible:_R_ithanpfn5tlb_:content" aria-expanded="false"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-code icon icon--size_sm" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m16 18 6-6-6-6"></path><path d="m8 6-6 6 6 6"></path></svg>Show Code</button></div></div>
<h2 id="guides" class="fs_1.5em mt_2em mb_1em lh_1.3333333 fw_700 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_800 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.875em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#guides"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Guides</h2>
<h3 id="close-behavior" class="fs_1.25em lh_1.6 mt_1.6em mb_0.6em fw_600 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_700 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.9em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#close-behavior"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Close Behavior</h3>
<ul class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em ps_1.625em li-t_disc [&amp;_&gt;_li]:ps_0.375em [&amp;_&gt;_li]:[&amp;::marker]:c_fg.subtle [&amp;_&gt;_li_p]:mt_0.75em [&amp;_&gt;_li_p]:mb_0.75em [&amp;_&gt;_li_&gt;_p:first-child]:mt_1.25em [&amp;_&gt;_li_&gt;_p:last-child]:mb_1.25em [&amp;_ul,_&amp;_ol]:mt_0.75em [&amp;_ul,_&amp;_ol]:mb_0.75em">
<li class="mt_0.5em mb_0.5em"><code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">closeOnEscape={false}</code> - Prevent closing on <kbd>Escape</kbd></li>
<li class="mt_0.5em mb_0.5em"><code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">closeOnInteractOutside={false}</code> - Prevent closing on outside click</li>
</ul>
<p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500">For conditional control, use <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">onEscapeKeyDown</code> or <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">onInteractOutside</code> with <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">e.preventDefault()</code>.</p>
<h3 id="z-index-stacking" class="fs_1.25em lh_1.6 mt_1.6em mb_0.6em fw_600 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_700 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.9em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#z-index-stacking"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Z-Index Stacking</h3>
<p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500">Use the <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">--layer-index</code> CSS variable for z-index management of stacked dialogs:</p>
<pre class="fs_0.875em lh_1.7142857 mt_1.7142857em mb_1.7142857em bdr_0.375rem p_4 color-scheme_dark [&amp;_code]:bg-c_transparent [&amp;_code]:bd-w_0 [&amp;_code]:bdr_0 [&amp;_code]:p_0 [&amp;_code]:fw_inherit [&amp;_code]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_inherit [&amp;_code]:ff_inherit [&amp;_code]:lh_inherit shiki github-dark-default" style="background-color:#0d1117;color:#e6edf3" tabindex="0"><code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2"><span class="line"><span style="color:#E6EDF3">[</span><span style="color:#79C0FF">data-part</span><span style="color:#FF7B72">=</span><span style="color:#A5D6FF">&#x27;content&#x27;</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">] {</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#79C0FF">  z-index</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">: </span><span style="color:#79C0FF">calc</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">(</span><span style="color:#79C0FF">var</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">(</span><span style="color:#FFA657">--layer-index</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">));</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E6EDF3">}</span></span></code></pre>
<h3 id="dynamic-imports" class="fs_1.25em lh_1.6 mt_1.6em mb_0.6em fw_600 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_700 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.9em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#dynamic-imports"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Dynamic Imports</h3>
<p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500">When using <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">lazyMount</code> with <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">React.lazy</code> or Next.js <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">dynamic</code>, wrap the imported component in <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">Suspense</code>:</p>
<pre class="fs_0.875em lh_1.7142857 mt_1.7142857em mb_1.7142857em bdr_0.375rem p_4 color-scheme_dark [&amp;_code]:bg-c_transparent [&amp;_code]:bd-w_0 [&amp;_code]:bdr_0 [&amp;_code]:p_0 [&amp;_code]:fw_inherit [&amp;_code]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_inherit [&amp;_code]:ff_inherit [&amp;_code]:lh_inherit shiki github-dark-default" style="background-color:#0d1117;color:#e6edf3" tabindex="0"><code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2"><span class="line"><span style="color:#FF7B72">import</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3"> { Dialog } </span><span style="color:#FF7B72">from</span><span style="color:#A5D6FF"> &#x27;@ark-ui/react/dialog&#x27;</span></span>

<span class="line"></span>

<span class="line"><span style="color:#E6EDF3">  &lt;</span><span style="color:#7EE787">Dialog.Root</span><span style="color:#79C0FF"> lazyMount</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">&gt;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E6EDF3">    &lt;</span><span style="color:#7EE787">Dialog.Trigger</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">&gt;Open&lt;/</span><span style="color:#7EE787">Dialog.Trigger</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">&gt;</span></span>

<h2 id="api-reference" class="fs_1.5em mt_2em mb_1em lh_1.3333333 fw_700 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_800 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.875em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#api-reference"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>API Reference</h2>

<h3 id="context-1" class="fs_1.25em lh_1.6 mt_1.6em mb_0.6em fw_600 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_700 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.9em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#context-1"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Context</h3>
<h3 class="text text--variant_heading text--size_xl">API</h3><div class="bd-w_1px bdr_lg ov-x_auto my_8 not-prose"><table class="bd_0 table__root table__root--size_sm table__root--variant_outline"><thead class="table__head table__head--size_sm table__head--variant_outline"><tr class="table__row table__row--size_sm table__row--variant_outline"><th class="px_4 bg_gray.2 h_10 table__header table__header--size_sm table__header--variant_outline">Property</th><th class="px_4 bg_gray.2 h_10 table__header table__header--size_sm table__header--variant_outline">Type</th></tr></thead><tbody class="table__body table__body--size_sm table__body--variant_outline"><tr class="table__row table__row--size_sm table__row--variant_outline"><td class="w_36 px_4 py_2 va_top table__cell table__cell--size_sm table__cell--variant_outline"><code class="code code--size_sm code--variant_outline c_colorPalette.default">open</code></td><td class="px_4 py_2 va_top table__cell table__cell--size_sm table__cell--variant_outline"><div class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_start gap_1"><code class="code code--size_sm code--variant_outline">boolean</code><p class="text">Whether the dialog is open</p></div></td></tr><tr class="table__row table__row--size_sm table__row--variant_outline"><td class="w_36 px_4 py_2 va_top table__cell table__cell--size_sm table__cell--variant_outline"><code class="code code--size_sm code--variant_outline c_colorPalette.default">setOpen</code></td><td class="px_4 py_2 va_top table__cell table__cell--size_sm table__cell--variant_outline"><div class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_start gap_1"><code class="code code--size_sm code--variant_outline">(open: boolean) =&gt; void</code><p class="text">Function to open or close the dialog</p></div></td></tr></tbody></table></div>
<h2 id="accessibility" class="fs_1.5em mt_2em mb_1em lh_1.3333333 fw_700 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_800 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.875em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#accessibility"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Accessibility</h2>
<p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500">Complies with the <a target="_blank" rel="noopener" href="https://www.w3.org/WAI/ARIA/apg/patterns/dialog-modal/" class="link">Dialog WAI-ARIA design pattern</a>.</p>
<h3 id="keyboard-support" class="fs_1.25em lh_1.6 mt_1.6em mb_0.6em fw_600 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_700 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.9em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#keyboard-support"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Keyboard Support</h3>
<div class="bd-w_1px bdr_lg ov-x_auto not-prose"><table class="bd_0 table__root table__root--size_sm table__root--variant_outline"><thead class="table__head table__head--size_sm table__head--variant_outline"><tr class="table__row table__row--size_sm table__row--variant_outline"><th class="px_4 bg_gray.2 h_10 table__header table__header--size_sm table__header--variant_outline">Key</th><th class="px_4 bg_gray.2 h_10 table__header table__header--size_sm table__header--variant_outline">Description</th></tr></thead><tbody class="table__body table__body--size_sm table__body--variant_outline"><tr class="table__row table__row--size_sm table__row--variant_outline"><td class="px_4 py_2 table__cell table__cell--size_sm table__cell--variant_outline"><div class="d_flex ai_center gap_1 flex-d_row"><kbd class="kbd kbd--size_sm c_gray.a11 px_1">Enter</kbd></div></td><td class="px_4 py_2 table__cell table__cell--size_sm table__cell--variant_outline">When focus is on the trigger, opens the dialog.</td></tr><tr class="table__row table__row--size_sm table__row--variant_outline"><td class="px_4 py_2 table__cell table__cell--size_sm table__cell--variant_outline"><div class="d_flex ai_center gap_1 flex-d_row"><kbd class="kbd kbd--size_sm c_gray.a11 px_1">Tab</kbd></div></td><td class="px_4 py_2 table__cell table__cell--size_sm table__cell--variant_outline">Moves focus to the next focusable element within the content. Focus is trapped within the dialog.</td></tr><tr class="table__row table__row--size_sm table__row--variant_outline"><td class="px_4 py_2 table__cell table__cell--size_sm table__cell--variant_outline"><div class="d_flex ai_center gap_1 flex-d_row"><kbd class="kbd kbd--size_sm c_gray.a11 px_1">Shift + Tab</kbd></div></td><td class="px_4 py_2 table__cell table__cell--size_sm table__cell--variant_outline">Moves focus to the previous focusable element. Focus is trapped within the dialog.</td></tr><tr class="table__row table__row--size_sm table__row--variant_outline"><td class="px_4 py_2 table__cell table__cell--size_sm table__cell--variant_outline"><div class="d_flex ai_center gap_1 flex-d_row"><kbd class="kbd kbd--size_sm c_gray.a11 px_1">Esc</kbd></div></td><td class="px_4 py_2 table__cell table__cell--size_sm table__cell--variant_outline">Closes the dialog and moves focus to trigger or the defined final focus element</td></tr></tbody></table></div></article><div class="d_flex flex-d_column-reverse    \u003c/Dialog.Positioner\u003e\n  \u003c/Portal\u003e\n\u003c/Dialog.Root\u003e\n\n```\n\n### Controlled\n\nManage the dialog state using the `open` and `onOpenChange` props.\n\n**Example: controlled**\n\n#### React\n\n```tsx\nimport { Dialog } from '@ark-ui/react/dialog'\nimport { Portal } from '@ark-ui/react/portal'\nimport { XIcon } from 'lucide-react'\nimport { useState } from 'react'\nimport button from 'styles/button.module.css'\nimport styles from 'styles/dialog.module.css'\n\nexport const Controlled = () =\u003e {\n  const [open, setOpen] = useState(false)\n  return (\n    \u003cDialog.Root open={open} onOpenChange={(e) =\u003e setOpen(e.open)}\u003e\n      \u003cDialog.Trigger className={button.Root}\u003eOpen Dialog\u003c/Dialog.Trigger\u003e\n      \u003cPortal\u003e\n        \u003cDialog.Backdrop className={styles.Backdrop} /\u003e\n        \u003cDialog.Positioner className={styles.Positioner}\u003e\n          \u003cDialog.Content className={styles.Content}\u003e\n            \u003cDialog.CloseTrigger className={styles.CloseTrigger}\u003e\n              \u003cXIcon /\u003e\n            \u003c/Dialog.CloseTrigger\u003e\n            \u003cDialog.Title className={styles.Title}\u003eSession Settings\u003c/Dialog.Title\u003e\n            \u003cDialog.Description className={styles.Description}\u003e\n              Manage your session preferences and security options.\n            \u003c/Dialog.Description\u003e\n          \u003c/Dialog.Content\u003e\n        \u003c/Dialog.Positioner\u003e\n      \u003c/Portal\u003e\n    \u003c/Dialog.Root\u003e\n  )\n}\n\n```\n\n#### Solid\n\n```tsx\nimport { Dialog } from '@ark-ui/solid/dialog'\nimport { XIcon } from 'lucide-solid'\nimport { createSignal } from 'solid-js'\nimport { Portal } from 'solid-js/web'\nimport button from 'styles/button.module.css'\nimport styles from 'styles/dialog.module.css'\n\nexport const Controlled = () =\u003e {\n  const [open, setOpen] = createSignal(false)\n\n  return (\n    \u003cDialog.Root open={open()} onOpenChange={(e) =\u003e setOpen(e.open)}\u003e\n      \u003cDialog.Trigger class={button.Root}\u003eOpen Dialog\u003c/Dialog.Trigger\u003e\n      \u003cPortal\u003e\n        \u003cDialog.Backdrop class={styles.Backdrop} /\u003e\n        \u003cDialog.Positioner class={styles.Positioner}\u003e\n          \u003cDialog.Content class={styles.Content}\u003e\n            \u003cDialog.CloseTrigger class={styles.CloseTrigger}\u003e\n              \u003cXIcon /\u003e\n            \u003c/Dialog.CloseTrigger\u003e\n            \u003cDialog.Title class={styles.Title}\u003eSession Settings\u003c/Dialog.Title\u003e\n            \u003cDialog.Description class={styles.Description}\u003e\n              Manage your session preferences and security options.\n            \u003c/Dialog.Description\u003e\n          \u003c/Dialog.Content\u003e\n        \u003c/Dialog.Positioner\u003e\n      \u003c/Portal\u003e\n    \u003c/Dialog.Root\u003e\n  )\n}\n\n```\n\n#### Vue\n\n```vue\n\u003cscript setup lang=\"ts\"\u003e\nimport { Dialog } from '@ark-ui/vue/dialog'\nimport { XIcon } from 'lucide-vue-next'\nimport { ref } from 'vue'\nimport button from 'styles/button.module.css'\nimport styles from 'styles/dialog.module.css'\n\nconst open = ref(false)\n\u003c/script\u003e\n\n\u003ctemplate\u003e\n  \u003cbutton :class=\"button.Root\" @click=\"() =\u003e (open = true)\"\u003eToggle\u003c/button\u003e\n  \u003cDialog.Root v-model:open=\"open\"\u003e\n    \u003cTeleport to=\"body\"\u003e\n      \u003cDialog.Backdrop :class=\"styles.Backdrop\" /\u003e\n      \u003cDialog.Positioner :class=\"styles.Positioner\"\u003e\n        \u003cDialog.Content :class=\"styles.Content\"\u003e\n          \u003cDialog.CloseTrigger :class=\"styles.CloseTrigger\"\u003e\n            \u003cXIcon /\u003e\n          \u003c/Dialog.CloseTrigger\u003e\n          \u003cDialog.Title :class=\"styles.Title\"\u003eSession Settings\u003c/Dialog.Title\u003e\n          \u003cDialog.Description :class=\"styles.Description\"\u003e\n            Manage your session preferences and security options.\n          \u003c/Dialog.Description\u003e\n        \u003c/Dialog.Content\u003e\n      \u003c/Dialog.Positioner\u003e\n    \u003c/Teleport\u003e\n  \u003c/Dialog.Root\u003e\n\u003c/template\u003e\n\n```\n\n#### Svelte\n\n```svelte\n\u003cscript lang=\"ts\"\u003e\n  import { Dialog } from '@ark-ui/svelte/dialog'\n  import { Portal } from '@ark-ui/svelte/portal'\n  import { XIcon } from 'lucide-svelte'\n  import button from 'styles/button.module.css'\n  import styles from 'styles/dialog.module.css'\n\n  let open = $state(false)\n\u003c/script\u003e\n\n\u003cbutton type=\"button\" class={button.Root} onclick={() =\u003e (open = !open)}\u003eToggle\u003c/button\u003e\n\u003cDialog.Root bind:open\u003e\n  \u003cPortal\u003e\n    \u003cDialog.Backdrop class={styles.Backdrop} /\u003e\n    \u003cDialog.Positioner class={styles.Positioner}\u003e\n      \u003cDialog.Content class={styles.Content}\u003e\n        \u003cDialog.CloseTrigger class={styles.CloseTrigger}\u003e\n          \u003cXIcon /\u003e\n        \u003c/Dialog.CloseTrigger\u003e\n        \u003cDialog.Title class={styles.Title}\u003eSession Settings\u003c/Dialog.Title\u003e\n        \u003cDialog.Description class={styles.Description}\u003e\n          Manage your session preferences and security options.\n        \u003c/Dialog.Description\u003e\n      \u003c/Dialog.Content\u003e\n    \u003c/Dialog.Positioner\u003e\n  \u003c/Portal\u003e\n\u003c/Dialog.Root\u003e\n\n```\n\n### Root Provider\n\nAn alternative way to control the dialog is to use the `RootProvider` component and the `useDialog` hook. This way you\ncan access the state and methods from outside the component.\n\n**Example: root-provider**\n\n#### React\n\n```tsx\nimport { Dialog, useDialog } from '@ark-ui/react/dialog'\nimport { Portal } from '@ark-ui/react/portal'\nimport { XIcon } from 'lucide-react'\nimport button from 'styles/button.module.css'\nimport styles from 'styles/dialog.module.css'\n\nexport const RootProvider = () =\u003e {\n  const dialog = useDialog()\n\n  return (\n    \u003cdiv className=\"stack\"\u003e\n      \u003cbutton className={button.Root} onClick={() =\u003e dialog.setOpen(true)}\u003e\n        Dialog is {dialog.open ? 'open' : 'closed'}\n      \u003c/button\u003e\n      \u003cDialog.RootProvider value={dialog}\u003e\n        \u003cPortal\u003e\n          \u003cDialog.Backdrop className={styles.Backdrop} /\u003e\n          \u003cDialog.Positioner className={styles.Positioner}\u003e\n            \u003cDialog.Content className={styles.Content}\u003e\n              \u003cDialog.CloseTrigger className={styles.CloseTrigger}\u003e\n                \u003cXIcon /\u003e\n              \u003c/Dialog.CloseTrigger\u003e\n              \u003cDialog.Title className={styles.Title}\u003eControlled Externally\u003c/Dialog.Title\u003e\n              \u003cDialog.Description className={styles.Description}\u003e\n                This dialog is controlled via the useDialog hook.\n              \u003c/Dialog.Description\u003e\n            \u003c/Dialog.Content\u003e\n          \u003c/Dialog.Positioner\u003e\n        \u003c/Portal\u003e\n      \u003c/Dialog.RootProvider\u003e\n    \u003c/div\u003e\n  )\n}\n\n```\n\n#### Solid\n\n```tsx\nimport { Dialog, useDialog } from '@ark-ui/solid/dialog'\nimport { XIcon } from 'lucide-solid'\nimport { Portal } from 'solid-js/web'\nimport button from 'styles/button.module.css'\nimport styles from 'styles/dialog.module.css'\n\nexport const RootProvider = () =\u003e {\n  const dialog = useDialog()\n\n  return (\n    \u003c\u003e\n      \u003cbutton class={button.Root} onClick={() =\u003e dialog().setOpen(true)}\u003e\n        Open\n      \u003c/button\u003e\n\n      \u003cDialog.RootProvider value={dialog}\u003e\n        \u003cPortal\u003e\n          \u003cDialog.Backdrop class={styles.Backdrop} /\u003e\n          \u003cDialog.Positioner class={styles.Positioner}\u003e\n            \u003cDialog.Content class={styles.Content}\u003e\n              \u003cDialog.CloseTrigger class={styles.CloseTrigger}\u003e\n                \u003cXIcon /\u003e\n              \u003c/Dialog.CloseTrigger\u003e\n              \u003cDialog.Title class={styles.Title}\u003eAccount Settings\u003c/Dialog.Title\u003e\n              \u003cDialog.Description class={styles.Description}\u003e\n                Manage your account preferences and security options.\n              \u003c/Dialog.Description\u003e\n            \u003c/Dialog.Content\u003e\n          \u003c/Dialog.Positioner\u003e\n        \u003c/Portal\u003e\n      \u003c/Dialog.RootProvider\u003e\n    \u003c/\u003e\n  )\n}\n\n```\n\n#### Vue\n\n```vue\n\u003cscript setup lang=\"ts\"\u003e\nimport { Dialog, useDialog } from '@ark-ui/vue/dialog'\nimport { XIcon } from 'lucide-vue-next'\nimport button from 'styles/button.module.css'\nimport styles from 'styles/dialog.module.css'\n\nconst dialog = useDialog()\n\u003c/script\u003e\n\n\u003ctemplate\u003e\n  \u003cbutton :class=\"button.Root\" @click=\"dialog.setOpen(true)\"\u003eOpen\u003c/button\u003e\n\n  \u003cDialog.RootProvider :value=\"dialog\"\u003e\n    \u003cTeleport to=\"body\"\u003e\n      \u003cDialog.Backdrop :class=\"styles.Backdrop\" /\u003e\n      \u003cDialog.Positioner :class=\"styles.Positioner\"\u003e\n        \u003cDialog.Content :class=\"styles.Content\"\u003e\n          \u003cDialog.CloseTrigger :class=\"styles.CloseTrigger\"\u003e\n            \u003cXIcon /\u003e\n          \u003c/Dialog.CloseTrigger\u003e\n          \u003cDialog.Title :class=\"styles.Title\"\u003eAccount Settings\u003c/Dialog.Title\u003e\n          \u003cDialog.Description :class=\"styles.Description\"\u003e\n            Manage your account preferences and security options.\n          \u003c/Dialog.Description\u003e\n        \u003c/Dialog.Content\u003e\n      \u003c/Dialog.Positioner\u003e\n    \u003c/Teleport\u003e\n  \u003c/Dialog.RootProvider\u003e\n\u003c/template\u003e\n\n```\n\n#### Svelte\n\n```svelte\n\u003cscript lang=\"ts\"\u003e\n  import { Dialog, useDialog } from '@ark-ui/svelte/dialog'\n  import { Portal } from '@ark-ui/svelte/portal'\n  import { XIcon } from 'lucide-svelte'\n  import button from 'styles/button.module.css'\n  import styles from 'styles/dialog.module.css'\n\n  const id = $props.id()\n\n  const dialog = useDialog({ id })\n\u003c/script\u003e\n\n\u003cbutton class={button.Root} onclick={() =\u003e dialog().setOpen(true)}\u003eOpen\u003c/button\u003e\n\n\u003cDialog.RootProvider value={dialog}\u003e\n  \u003cPortal\u003e\n    \u003cDialog.Backdrop class={styles.Backdrop} /\u003e\n    \u003cDialog.Positioner class={styles.Positioner}\u003e\n      \u003cDialog.Content class={styles.Content}\u003e\n        \u003cDialog.CloseTrigger class={styles.CloseTrigger}\u003e\n          \u003cXIcon /\u003e\n        \u003c/Dialog.CloseTrigger\u003e\n        \u003cDialog.Title class={styles.Title}\u003eAccount Settings\u003c/Dialog.Title\u003e\n        \u003cDialog.Description class={styles.Description}\u003e\n          Manage your account preferences and security options.\n        \u003c/Dialog.Description\u003e\n      \u003c/Dialog.Content\u003e\n    \u003c/Dialog.Positioner\u003e\n  \u003c/Portal\u003e\n\u003c/Dialog.RootProvider\u003e\n\n```\n\n### Alert Dialog\n\nFor critical confirmations or destructive actions, use `role=\"alertdialog\"`. Alert dialogs differ from regular dialogs\nin important ways:\n\n- **Automatic focus**: The close/cancel button receives focus when opened, prioritizing the safest action\n- **Requires explicit dismissal**: Cannot be closed by clicking outside, only via button clicks or Escape key\n\n**Example: alert-dialog**\n\n#### React\n\n```tsx\nimport { Dialog } from '@ark-ui/react/dialog'\nimport { Portal } from '@ark-ui/react/portal'\nimport button from 'styles/button.module.css'\nimport styles from 'styles/dialog.module.css'\n\nexport const AlertDialog = () =\u003e (\n  \u003cDialog.Root role=\"alertdialog\"\u003e\n    \u003cDialog.Trigger className={button.Root}\u003eDelete Account\u003c/Dialog.Trigger\u003e\n    \u003cPortal\u003e\n      \u003cDialog.Backdrop className={styles.Backdrop} /\u003e\n      \u003cDialog.Positioner className={styles.Positioner}\u003e\n        \u003cDialog.Content className={styles.Content}\u003e\n          \u003cDialog.Title className={styles.Title}\u003eAre you absolutely sure?\u003c/Dialog.Title\u003e\n          \u003cDialog.Description className={styles.Description}\u003e\n            This action cannot be undone. This will permanently delete your account and remove your data from our\n            servers.\n          \u003c/Dialog.Description\u003e\n          \u003cdiv className={styles.Actions}\u003e\n            \u003cDialog.CloseTrigger className={button.Root}\u003eCancel\u003c/Dialog.CloseTrigger\u003e\n            \u003cbutton className={button.Root} data-variant=\"solid\"\u003e\n              Delete Account\n            \u003c/button\u003e\n          \u003c/div\u003e\n        \u003c/Dialog.Content\u003e\n      \u003c/Dialog.Positioner\u003e\n    \u003c/Portal\u003e\n  \u003c/Dialog.Root\u003e\n)\n\n```\n\n#### Solid\n\n```tsx\nimport { Dialog } from '@ark-ui/solid/dialog'\nimport { XIcon } from 'lucide-solid'\nimport { Portal } from 'solid-js/web'\nimport button from 'styles/button.module.css'\nimport styles from 'styles/dialog.module.css'\n\nexport const AlertDialog = () =\u003e (\n  \u003cDialog.Root role=\"alertdialog\"\u003e\n    \u003cDialog.Trigger class={button.Root}\u003eDelete Account\u003c/Dialog.Trigger\u003e\n    \u003cPortal\u003e\n      \u003cDialog.Backdrop class={styles.Backdrop} /\u003e\n      \u003cDialog.Positioner class={styles.Positioner}\u003e\n        \u003cDialog.Content class={styles.Content}\u003e\n          \u003cDialog.CloseTrigger class={styles.CloseTrigger}\u003e\n            \u003cXIcon /\u003e\n          \u003c/Dialog.CloseTrigger\u003e\n          \u003cDialog.Title class={styles.Title}\u003eAre you absolutely sure?\u003c/Dialog.Title\u003e\n          \u003cDialog.Description class={styles.Description}\u003e\n            This action cannot be undone. This will permanently delete your account and remove your data from our\n            servers.\n          \u003c/Dialog.Description\u003e\n          \u003cdiv class={styles.Actions}\u003e\n            \u003cDialog.CloseTrigger class={button.Root}\u003eCancel\u003c/Dialog.CloseTrigger\u003e\n            \u003cbutton type=\"button\" class={button.Root}\u003e\n              Delete Account\n            \u003c/button\u003e\n          \u003c/div\u003e\n        \u003c/Dialog.Content\u003e\n      \u003c/Dialog.Positioner\u003e\n    \u003c/Portal\u003e\n  \u003c/Dialog.Root\u003e\n)\n\n```\n\n#### Vue\n\n```vue\n\u003cscript setup lang=\"ts\"\u003e\nimport { Dialog } from '@ark-ui/vue/dialog'\nimport { XIcon } from 'lucide-vue-next'\nimport button from 'styles/button.module.css'\nimport styles from 'styles/dialog.module.css'\n\u003c/script\u003e\n\n\u003ctemplate\u003e\n  \u003cDialog.Root role=\"alertdialog\"\u003e\n    \u003cDialog.Trigger :class=\"button.Root\"\u003eDelete Account\u003c/Dialog.Trigger\u003e\n    \u003cTeleport to=\"body\"\u003e\n      \u003cDialog.Backdrop :class=\"styles.Backdrop\" /\u003e\n      \u003cDialog.Positioner :class=\"styles.Positioner\"\u003e\n        \u003cDialog.Content :class=\"styles.Content\"\u003e\n          \u003cDialog.CloseTrigger :class=\"styles.CloseTrigger\"\u003e\n            \u003cXIcon /\u003e\n          \u003c/Dialog.CloseTrigger\u003e\n          \u003cDialog.Title :class=\"styles.Title\"\u003eAre you absolutely sure?\u003c/Dialog.Title\u003e\n          \u003cDialog.Description :class=\"styles.Description\"\u003e\n            This action cannot be undone. This will permanently delete your account and remove your data from our\n            servers.\n          \u003c/Dialog.Description\u003e\n          \u003cdiv :class=\"styles.Actions\"\u003e\n            \u003cDialog.CloseTrigger :class=\"button.Root\"\u003eCancel\u003c/Dialog.CloseTrigger\u003e\n            \u003cbutton type=\"button\" :class=\"button.Root\"\u003eDelete Account\u003c/button\u003e\n          \u003c/div\u003e\n        \u003c/Dialog.Content\u003e\n      \u003c/Dialog.Positioner\u003e\n    \u003c/Teleport\u003e\n  \u003c/Dialog.Root\u003e\n\u003c/template\u003e\n\n```\n\n#### Svelte\n\n```svelte\n\u003cscript lang=\"ts\"\u003e\n  import { Dialog } from '@ark-ui/svelte/dialog'\n  import { Portal } from '@ark-ui/svelte/portal'\n  import { XIcon } from 'lucide-svelte'\n  import button from 'styles/button.module.css'\n  import styles from 'styles/dialog.module.css'\n\u003c/script\u003e\n\n\u003cDialog.Root role=\"alertdialog\"\u003e\n  \u003cDialog.Trigger class={button.Root}\u003eDelete Account\u003c/Dialog.Trigger\u003e\n  \u003cPortal\u003e\n    \u003cDialog.Backdrop class={styles.Backdrop} /\u003e\n    \u003cDialog.Positioner class={styles.Positioner}\u003e\n      \u003cDialog.Content class={styles.Content}\u003e\n        \u003cDialog.CloseTrigger class={styles.CloseTrigger}\u003e\n          \u003cXIcon /\u003e\n        \u003c/Dialog.CloseTrigger\u003e\n        \u003cDialog.Title class={styles.Title}\u003eAre you absolutely sure?\u003c/Dialog.Title\u003e\n        \u003cDialog.Description class={styles.Description}\u003e\n          This action cannot be undone. This will permanently delete your account and remove your data from our servers.\n        \u003c/Dialog.Description\u003e\n        \u003cdiv class={styles.Actions}\u003e\n          \u003cDialog.CloseTrigger class={button.Root}\u003eCancel\u003c/Dialog.CloseTrigger\u003e\n          \u003cbutton type=\"button\" class={button.Root}\u003eDelete Account\u003c/button\u003e\n        \u003c/div\u003e\n      \u003c/Dialog.Content\u003e\n    \u003c/Dialog.Positioner\u003e\n  \u003c/Portal\u003e\n\u003c/Dialog.Root\u003e\n\n```\n\n### Lazy Mount\n\nUse `lazyMount` to render dialog content only when first opened. Combine with `unmountOnExit` to unmount when closed,\nfreeing up resources.\n\n**Example: lazy-mount**\n\n#### React\n\n```tsx\nimport { Dialog } from '@ark-ui/react/dialog'\nimport { Portal } from '@ark-ui/react/portal'\nimport { XIcon } from 'lucide-react'\nimport button from 'styles/button.module.css'\nimport styles from 'styles/dialog.module.css'\n\nexport const LazyMount = () =\u003e (\n  \u003cDialog.Root lazyMount unmountOnExit\u003e\n    \u003cDialog.Trigger className={button.Root}\u003eOpen Dialog\u003c/Dialog.Trigger\u003e\n    \u003cPortal\u003e\n      \u003cDialog.Backdrop className={styles.Backdrop} /\u003e\n      \u003cDialog.Positioner className={styles.Positioner}\u003e\n        \u003cDialog.Content className={styles.Content}\u003e\n          \u003cDialog.CloseTrigger className={styles.CloseTrigger}\u003e\n            \u003cXIcon /\u003e\n          \u003c/Dialog.CloseTrigger\u003e\n          \u003cDialog.Title className={styles.Title}\u003eLazy Loaded\u003c/Dialog.Title\u003e\n          \u003cDialog.Description className={styles.Description}\u003e\n            This dialog content is only mounted when opened and unmounts on close.\n          \u003c/Dialog.Description\u003e\n        \u003c/Dialog.Content\u003e\n      \u003c/Dialog.Positioner\u003e\n    \u003c/Portal\u003e\n  \u003c/Dialog.Root\u003e\n)\n\n```\n\n#### Solid\n\n```tsx\nimport { Dialog } from '@ark-ui/solid/dialog'\nimport { XIcon } from 'lucide-solid'\nimport { Portal } from 'solid-js/web'\nimport button from 'styles/button.module.css'\nimport styles from 'styles/dialog.module.css'\n\nexport const LazyMount = () =\u003e (\n  \u003cDialog.Root lazyMount unmountOnExit\u003e\n    \u003cDialog.Trigger class={button.Root}\u003eOpen Dialog\u003c/Dialog.Trigger\u003e\n    \u003cPortal\u003e\n      \u003cDialog.Backdrop class={styles.Backdrop} /\u003e\n      \u003cDialog.Positioner class={styles.Positioner}\u003e\n        \u003cDialog.Content class={styles.Content}\u003e\n          \u003cDialog.CloseTrigger class={styles.CloseTrigger}\u003e\n            \u003cXIcon /\u003e\n          \u003c/Dialog.CloseTrigger\u003e\n          \u003cDialog.Title class={styles.Title}\u003eLazy Mounted Dialog\u003c/Dialog.Title\u003e\n          \u003cDialog.Description class={styles.Description}\u003e\n            This dialog content is only mounted when opened and unmounted when closed.\n          \u003c/Dialog.Description\u003e\n        \u003c/Dialog.Content\u003e\n      \u003c/Dialog.Positioner\u003e\n    \u003c/Portal\u003e\n  \u003c/Dialog.Root\u003e\n)\n\n```\n\n#### Vue\n\n```vue\n\u003cscript setup lang=\"ts\"\u003e\nimport { \u003c/Dialog.Content\u003e\n      \u003c/Dialog.Positioner\u003e\n    \u003c/Teleport\u003e\n  \u003c/Dialog.Root\u003e\n\u003c/template\u003e\n\n```\n\n#### Svelte\n\n```svelte\n\u003cscript          This dialog content is only mounted when opened and unmounted when closed.\n        \u003c/Dialog.Description\u003e\n      \u003c/Dialog.Content\u003e\n    \u003c/Dialog.Positioner\u003e\n  \u003c/Portal\u003e\n\u003c/Dialog.Root\u003e\n\n```\n\n### Initial Focus\n\nUse `initialFocusEl` to control which element receives focus when the dialog opens.\n\n**Example: initial-focus**\n\n#### React\n\n```tsx\nimport { Dialog } from '@ark-ui/react/dialog'\nimport { Portal } from '@ark-ui/react/portal'\nimport { XIcon } from 'lucide-react'\nimport { useRef } from 'react'\nimport button from 'styles/button.module.css'\nimport field from 'styles/field.module.css'\nimport styles from 'styles/dialog.module.css'\n\nexport const InitialFocus = () =\u003e {\n  const inputRef = useRef\u003cHTMLInputElement\u003e(null)\n\n  return (\n    \u003cDialog.Root initialFocusEl={() =\u003e inputRef.current}\u003e\n      \u003cDialog.Trigger className={button.Root}\u003eOpen Dialog\u003c/Dialog.Trigger\u003e\n      \u003cPortal\u003e\n        \u003cDialog.Backdrop className={styles.Backdrop} /\u003e\n        \u003cDialog.Positioner className={styles.Positioner}\u003e\n          \u003cDialog.Content className={styles.Content}\u003e\n            \u003cDialog.CloseTrigger className={styles.CloseTrigger}\u003e\n              \u003cXIcon /\u003e\n            \u003c/Dialog.CloseTrigger\u003e\n            \u003cDialog.Title className={styles.Title}\u003eEdit Profile\u003c/Dialog.Title\u003e\n            \u003cDialog.Description className={styles.Description}\u003e\n              The first input will be focused when the dialog opens.\n            \u003c/Dialog.Description\u003e\n            \u003cdiv className={styles.Body}\u003e\n              \u003cinput ref={inputRef} className={field.Input} placeholder=\"Enter your name...\" /\u003e\n              \u003cinput className={field.Input} placeholder=\"Enter your email...\" /\u003e\n            \u003c/div\u003e\n          \u003c/Dialog.Content\u003e\n        \u003c/Dialog.Positioner\u003e\n      \u003c/Portal\u003e\n    \u003c/Dialog.Root\u003e\n  )\n}\n\n```\n\n#### Solid\n\n```tsx\nimport { Dialog } from '@ark-ui/solid/dialog'\nimport { XIcon } from 'lucide-solid'\nimport { Portal } from 'solid-js/web'\nimport button from 'styles/button.module.css'\nimport styles from 'styles/dialog.module.css'\n\nexport const InitialFocus = () =\u003e {\n  let inputRef: HTMLInputElement | undefined\n\n  return (\n    \u003cDialog.Root initialFocusEl={() =\u003e inputRef!}\u003e\n      \u003cDialog.Trigger class={button.Root}\u003eOpen Dialog\u003c/Dialog.Trigger\u003e\n      \u003cPortal\u003e\n        \u003cDialog.Backdrop class={styles.Backdrop} /\u003e\n        \u003cDialog.Positioner class={styles.Positioner}\u003e\n          \u003cDialog.Content class={styles.Content}\u003e\n            \u003cDialog.CloseTrigger class={styles.CloseTrigger}\u003e\n              \u003cXIcon /\u003e\n            \u003c/Dialog.CloseTrigger\u003e\n            \u003cDialog.Title class={styles.Title}\u003eEdit Profile\u003c/Dialog.Title\u003e\n            \u003cDialog.Description class={styles.Description}\u003e\n              The name input will be focused when this dialog opens.\n            \u003c/Dialog.Description\u003e\n            \u003cdiv class={styles.Body}\u003e\n              \u003cinput ref={inputRef} type=\"text\" placeholder=\"Enter your name\" /\u003e\n              \u003cinput type=\"email\" placeholder=\"Enter your email\" /\u003e\n            \u003c/div\u003e\n          \u003c/Dialog.Content\u003e\n        \u003c/Dialog.Positioner\u003e\n      \u003c/Portal\u003e\n    \u003c/Dialog.Root\u003e\n  )\n}\n\n```\n\n#### Vue\n\n```vue\n\u003cscript setup lang=\"ts\"\u003e\nimport { Dialog } from '@ark-ui/vue/dialog'\nimport { XIcon } from 'lucide-vue-next'\nimport { ref } from 'vue'\nimport button from 'styles/button.module.css'\nimport styles from 'styles/dialog.module.css'\n\nconst inputRef = ref\u003cHTMLInputElement | null\u003e(null)\n\u003c/script\u003e\n\n\u003ctemplate\u003e\n  \u003cDialog.Root :initial-focus-el=\"() =\u003e inputRef\"\u003e\n    \u003cDialog.Trigger :class=\"button.Root\"\u003eOpen Dialog\u003c/Dialog.Trigger\u003e\n    \u003cTeleport to=\"body\"\u003e\n      \u003cDialog.Backdrop :class=\"styles.Backdrop\" /\u003e\n      \u003cDialog.Positioner :class=\"styles.Positioner\"\u003e\n        \u003cDialog.Content :class=\"styles.Content\"\u003e\n          \u003cDialog.CloseTrigger :class=\"styles.CloseTrigger\"\u003e\n            \u003cXIcon /\u003e\n          \u003c/Dialog.CloseTrigger\u003e\n          \u003cDialog.Title :class=\"styles.Title\"\u003eEdit Profile\u003c/Dialog.Title\u003e\n          \u003cDialog.Description :class=\"styles.Description\"\u003e\n            The name input will be focused when this dialog opens.\n          \u003c/Dialog.Description\u003e\n          \u003cdiv :class=\"styles.Body\"\u003e\n            \u003cinput ref=\"inputRef\" type=\"text\" placeholder=\"Enter your name\" /\u003e\n            \u003cinput type=\"email\" placeholder=\"Enter your email\" /\u003e\n          \u003c/div\u003e\n        \u003c/Dialog.Content\u003e\n      \u003c/Dialog.Positioner\u003e\n    \u003c/Teleport\u003e\n  \u003c/Dialog.Root\u003e\n\u003c/template\u003e\n\n```\n\n#### Svelte\n\n```svelte\n\u003cscript lang=\"ts\"\u003e\n  import { Dialog } from '@ark-ui/svelte/dialog'\n  import { Portal } from '@ark-ui/svelte/portal'\n  import { XIcon } from 'lucide-svelte'\n  import button from 'styles/button.module.css'\n  import styles from 'styles/dialog.module.css'\n\n  let inputRef: HTMLInputElement\n\u003c/script\u003e\n\n\u003cDialog.Root initialFocusEl={() =\u003e inputRef}\u003e\n  \u003cDialog.Trigger class={button.Root}\u003eOpen Dialog\u003c/Dialog.Trigger\u003e\n  \u003cPortal\u003e\n    \u003cDialog.Backdrop class={styles.Backdrop} /\u003e\n    \u003cDialog.Positioner class={styles.Positioner}\u003e\n      \u003cDialog.Content class={styles.Content}\u003e\n        \u003cDialog.CloseTrigger class={styles.CloseTrigger}\u003e\n          \u003cXIcon /\u003e\n        \u003c/Dialog.CloseTrigger\u003e\n        \u003cDialog.Title class={styles.Title}\u003eEdit Profile\u003c/Dialog.Title\u003e\n        \u003cDialog.Description class={styles.Description}\u003e\n          The name input will be focused when this dialog opens.\n        \u003c/Dialog.Description\u003e\n        \u003cdiv class={styles.Body}\u003e\n          \u003cinput bind:this={inputRef} type=\"text\" placeholder=\"Enter your name\" /\u003e\n          \u003cinput type=\"email\" placeholder=\"Enter your email\" /\u003e\n        \u003c/div\u003e\n      \u003c/Dialog.Content\u003e\n    \u003c/Dialog.Positioner\u003e\n  \u003c/Portal\u003e\n\u003c/Dialog.Root\u003e\n\n```\n\n### Final Focus\n\nUse `finalFocusEl` to control which element receives focus when the dialog closes. Defaults to the trigger element.\n\n**Example: final-focus**\n\n#### React\n\n```tsx\nimport { Dialog } from '@ark-ui/react/dialog'\nimport { Portal } from '@ark-ui/react/portal'\nimport { XIcon } from 'lucide-react'\nimport { useRef } from 'react'\nimport button from 'styles/button.module.css'\nimport styles from 'styles/dialog.module.css'\n\nexport const FinalFocus = () =\u003e {\n  const finalRef = useRef\u003cHTMLButtonElement\u003e(null)\n\n  return (\n    \u003cdiv className=\"stack\"\u003e\n      \u003cbutton className={button.Root} ref={finalRef}\u003e\n        I will receive focus when dialog closes\n      \u003c/button\u003e\n      \u003cDialog.Root finalFocusEl={() =\u003e finalRef.current}\u003e\n        \u003cDialog.Trigger className={button.Root}\u003eOpen Dialog\u003c/Dialog.Trigger\u003e\n        \u003cPortal\u003e\n          \u003cDialog.Backdrop className={styles.Backdrop} /\u003e\n          \u003cDialog.Positioner className={styles.Positioner}\u003e\n            \u003cDialog.Content className={styles.Content}\u003e\n              \u003cDialog.CloseTrigger className={styles.CloseTrigger}\u003e\n                \u003cXIcon /\u003e\n              \u003c/Dialog.CloseTrigger\u003e\n              \u003cDialog.Title className={styles.Title}\u003eFocus Redirect\u003c/Dialog.Title\u003e\n              \u003cDialog.Description className={styles.Description}\u003e\n                When this dialog closes, focus will return to the button above instead of the trigger.\n              \u003c/Dialog.Description\u003e\n            \u003c/Dialog.Content\u003e\n          \u003c/Dialog.Positioner\u003e\n        \u003c/Portal\u003e\n      \u003c/Dialog.Root\u003e\n    \u003c/div\u003e\n  )\n}\n\n```\n\n#### Solid\n\n```tsx\nimport { Dialog } from '@ark-ui/solid/dialog'\nimport { XIcon } from 'lucide-solid'\nimport { Portal } from 'solid-js/web'\nimport button from 'styles/button.module.css'\nimport styles from 'styles/dialog.module.css'\n\nexport const FinalFocus = () =\u003e {\n  let buttonRef: HTMLButtonElement | undefined\n\n  return (\n    \u003c\u003e\n      \u003cbutton ref={buttonRef} class={button.Root}\u003e\n        Focus Target\n      \u003c/button\u003e\n      \u003cDialog.Root finalFocusEl={() =\u003e buttonRef!}\u003e\n        \u003cDialog.Trigger class={button.Root}\u003eOpen Dialog\u003c/Dialog.Trigger\u003e\n        \u003cPortal\u003e\n          \u003cDialog.Backdrop class={styles.Backdrop} /\u003e\n          \u003cDialog.Positioner class={styles.Positioner}\u003e\n            \u003cDialog.Content class={styles.Content}\u003e\n              \u003cDialog.CloseTrigger class={styles.CloseTrigger}\u003e\n                \u003cXIcon /\u003e\n              \u003c/Dialog.CloseTrigger\u003e\n              \u003cDialog.Title class={styles.Title}\u003eCustom Focus Return\u003c/Dialog.Title\u003e\n              \u003cDialog.Description class={styles.Description}\u003e\n                When this dialog closes, focus will return to the \"Focus Target\" button instead of the trigger.\n              \u003c/Dialog.Description\u003e\n            \u003c/Dialog.Content\u003e\n          \u003c/Dialog.Positioner\u003e\n        \u003c/Portal\u003e\n      \u003c/Dialog.Root\u003e\n    \u003c/\u003e\n  )\n}\n\n```\n\n#### Vue\n\n```vue\n\u003cscript setup lang=\"ts\"\u003e\nimport { Dialog } from '@ark-ui/vue/dialog'\nimport { XIcon } from 'lucide-vue-next'\nimport { ref } from 'vue'\nimport button from 'styles/button.module.css'\nimport styles from 'styles/dialog.module.css'\n\nconst buttonRef = ref\u003cHTMLButtonElement | null\u003e(null)\n\u003c/script\u003e\n\n\u003ctemplate\u003e\n  \u003cbutton ref=\"buttonRef\" :class=\"button.Root\"\u003eFocus Target\u003c/button\u003e\n  \u003cDialog.Root :final-focus-el=\"() =\u003e buttonRef\"\u003e\n    \u003cDialog.Trigger :class=\"button.Root\"\u003eOpen Dialog\u003c/Dialog.Trigger\u003e\n    \u003cTeleport to=\"body\"\u003e\n      \u003cDialog.Backdrop :class=\"styles.Backdrop\" /\u003e\n      \u003cDialog.Positioner :class=\"styles.Positioner\"\u003e\n        \u003cDialog.Content :class=\"styles.Content\"\u003e\n          \u003cDialog.CloseTrigger :class=\"styles.CloseTrigger\"\u003e\n            \u003cXIcon /\u003e\n          \u003c/Dialog.CloseTrigger\u003e\n          \u003cDialog.Title :class=\"styles.Title\"\u003eCustom Focus Return\u003c/Dialog.Title\u003e\n          \u003cDialog.Description :class=\"styles.Description\"\u003e\n            When this dialog closes, focus will return to the \"Focus Target\" button instead of the trigger.\n          \u003c/Dialog.Description\u003e\n        \u003c/Dialog.Content\u003e\n      \u003c/Dialog.Positioner\u003e\n    \u003c/Teleport\u003e\n  \u003c/Dialog.Root\u003e\n\u003c/template\u003e\n\n```\n\n#### Svelte\n\n```svelte\n\u003cscript lang=\"ts\"\u003e\n  import { Dialog } from '@ark-ui/svelte/dialog'\n  import { Portal } from '@ark-ui/svelte/portal'\n  import { XIcon } from 'lucide-svelte'\n  import button from 'styles/button.module.css'\n  import styles from 'styles/dialog.module.css'\n\n  let buttonRef: HTMLButtonElement\n\u003c/script\u003e\n\n\u003cbutton bind:this={buttonRef} class={button.Root}\u003eFocus Target\u003c/button\u003e\n\u003cDialog.Root finalFocusEl={() =\u003e buttonRef}\u003e\n  \u003cDialog.Trigger class={button.Root}\u003eOpen Dialog\u003c/Dialog.Trigger\u003e\n  \u003cPortal\u003e\n    \u003cDialog.Backdrop class={styles.Backdrop} /\u003e\n    \u003cDialog.Positioner class={styles.Positioner}\u003e\n      \u003cDialog.Content class={styles.Content}\u003e\n        \u003cDialog.CloseTrigger class={styles.CloseTrigger}\u003e\n          \u003cXIcon /\u003e\n        \u003c/Dialog.CloseTrigger\u003e\n        \u003cDialog.Title class={styles.Title}\u003eCustom Focus Return\u003c/Dialog.Title\u003e\n        \u003cDialog.Description class={styles.Description}\u003e\n          When this dialog closes, focus will return to the \"Focus Target\" button instead of the trigger.\n        \u003c/Dialog.Description\u003e\n      \u003c/Dialog.Content\u003e\n    \u003c/Dialog.Positioner\u003e\n  \u003c/Portal\u003e\n\u003c/Dialog.Root\u003e\n\n```\n\n### Non-Modal\n\nUse `modal={false}` to allow interaction with elements outside the dialog. Disables focus trapping and scroll\nprevention.\n\n**Example: non-modal**\n\n#### React\n\n```tsx\nimport { Dialog } from '@ark-ui/react/dialog'\nimport { Portal } from '@ark-ui/react/portal'\nimport { XIcon } from 'lucide-react'\nimport button from 'styles/button.module.css'\nimport styles from 'styles/dialog.module.css'\n\nexport const NonModal = () =\u003e (\n  \u003cDialog.Root modal={false}\u003e\n    \u003cDialog.Trigger className={button.Root}\u003eOpen Non-Modal Dialog\u003c/Dialog.Trigger\u003e\n    \u003cPortal\u003e\n      \u003cDialog.Backdrop className={styles.Backdrop} /\u003e\n      \u003cDialog.Positioner className={styles.Positioner}\u003e\n        \u003cDialog.Content className={styles.Content}\u003e\n          \u003cDialog.CloseTrigger className={styles.CloseTrigger}\u003e\n            \u003cXIcon /\u003e\n          \u003c/Dialog.CloseTrigger\u003e\n          \u003cDialog.Title className={styles.Title}\u003eNon-Modal Dialog\u003c/Dialog.Title\u003e\n          \u003cDialog.Description className={styles.Description}\u003e\n            This dialog allows interaction with elements outside. You can click buttons, select text, and interact with\n            the page behind it.\n          \u003c/Dialog.Description\u003e\n        \u003c/Dialog.Content\u003e\n      \u003c/Dialog.Positioner\u003e\n    \u003c/Portal\u003e\n  \u003c/Dialog.Root\u003e\n)\n\n```\n\n#### Solid\n\n```tsx\nimport { Dialog } from '@ark-ui/solid/dialog'\nimport { XIcon } from 'lucide-solid'\nimport { Portal } from 'solid-js/web'\nimport button from 'styles/button.module.css'\nimport styles from 'styles/dialog.module.css'\n\nexport const NonModal = () =\u003e (\n  \u003cDialog.Root modal={false}\u003e\n    \u003cDialog.Trigger class={button.Root}\u003eOpen Non-Modal\u003c/Dialog.Trigger\u003e\n    \u003cPortal\u003e\n      \u003cDialog.Backdrop class={styles.Backdrop} /\u003e\n      \u003cDialog.Positioner class={styles.Positioner}\u003e\n        \u003cDialog.Content class={styles.Content}\u003e\n          \u003cDialog.CloseTrigger class={styles.CloseTrigger}\u003e\n            \u003cXIcon /\u003e\n          \u003c/Dialog.CloseTrigger\u003e\n          \u003cDialog.Title class={styles.Title}\u003eNon-Modal \u003c/Dialog.Description\u003e\n        \u003c/Dialog.Content\u003e\n      \u003c/Dialog.Positioner\u003e\n    \u003c/Portal\u003e\n  \u003c/Dialog.Root\u003e\n)\n\n```\n\n#### Vue\n\n```vue\n\u003cscript setup lang=\"ts\"\u003e\nimport { Dialog } from '@ark-ui/vue/dialog'\nimport { XIcon } from 'lucide-vue-next'\nimport button from 'styles/button.module.css'\nimport styles     \u003cDialog.CloseTrigger class={styles.CloseTrigger}\u003e\n          \u003cXIcon /\u003e\n        \u003c/Dialog.CloseTrigger\u003e\n        \u003cDialog.Title class={styles.Title}\u003eNon-Modal \u003c/Dialog.Description\u003e\n      \u003c/Dialog.Content\u003e\n    \u003c/Dialog.Positioner\u003e\n  \u003c/Portal\u003e\n\u003c/Dialog.Root\u003e\n\n```\n\n### Inside Scroll\n\nMake the content area scrollable while keeping header and footer fixed using `maxHeight` and `overflow: auto`.\n\n**Example: inside-scroll**\n\n#### React\n\n```tsx\nimport { Dialog } from '@ark-ui/react/dialog'\nimport { Portal } from '@ark-ui/react/portal'\nimport { XIcon } from 'lucide-react'\nimport button from 'styles/button.module.css'\nimport styles from 'styles/dialog.module.css'\n\nexport const InsideScroll = () =\u003e (\n  \u003cDialog.Root\u003e\n    \u003cDialog.Trigger className={button.Root}\u003eOpen Dialog\u003c/Dialog.Trigger\u003e\n    \u003cPortal\u003e\n      \u003cDialog.Backdrop className={styles.Backdrop} /\u003e\n      \u003cDialog.Positioner className={styles.Positioner}\u003e\n        \u003cDialog.Content className={styles.Content} style={{ maxHeight: 'min(32rem, calc(100vh - 4rem))' }}\u003e\n          \u003cDialog.CloseTrigger className={styles.CloseTrigger}\u003e\n            \u003cXIcon /\u003e\n          \u003c/Dialog.CloseTrigger\u003e\n          \u003cDialog.Title className={styles.Title}\u003eTerms of Service\u003c/Dialog.Title\u003e\n          \u003cDialog.Description className={styles.Description}\u003e\n            Please review our terms before continuing.\n          \u003c/Dialog.Description\u003e\n          \u003cdiv className={styles.ScrollContainer}\u003e\n            {CONTENT_SECTIONS.map((item) =\u003e (\n              \u003csection key={item.title} className={styles.ScrollSection}\u003e\n                \u003ch3\u003e{item.title}\u003c/h3\u003e\n                \u003cp\u003e{item.body}\u003c/p\u003e\n              \u003c/section\u003e\n            ))}\n          \u003c/div\u003e\n          \u003cdiv className={styles.Actions}\u003e\n
